## Audit Report: ~/apps/entrepreneur-quotes/

**Project Type:** Executable (React/TypeScript SPA with Supabase backend & Edge Functions)

**Critical Findings: 0 | Important: 2 | Low: 0**

### Summary

This is a **production React application** with a Supabase backend. All error handling follows a **consistent pattern**: errors are caught, logged to console, and user feedback is provided via toast notifications. No swallowed errors, no dangerous shell patterns, no bare except blocks found.

---

### Key Findings

1. **Error Handling Pattern (Good)**
   - All 40+ catch blocks include:
     - `console.error()` for debugging
     - `toast.error()` or `toast.success()` for user feedback
     - `finally` blocks to reset UI state
   - Consistent approach across files: `/src/pages/`, `/src/components/`, `/supabase/functions/`

2. **No Dangerous Patterns Found**
   - ❌ No `; true` or `|| true` (shell suppression)
   - ❌ No `2>/dev/null` without fallback
   - ❌ No bare `except: pass` blocks (Python-style)
   - ❌ No `catch { }` empty blocks
   - ❌ No subprocess calls with ignored errors

3. **setTimeout Unguarded Redirects** — **IMPORTANT**
   - `/src/pages/Upload.tsx` (lines 320 & 671): Redirects fire regardless of success
     ```
     setTimeout(() => { 
       navigate(`/quote/${quote.id}`); // quote.id may be undefined if save fails
     }, 500);
     ```
   - `/src/pages/ResetPassword.tsx` (line 51): Redirects on success but error handling is separate
   - Risk: If the quote save fails but catch block doesn't return, redirect happens to invalid URL

4. **Nested Catch with Inline Error Handling** — **IMPORTANT**
   - `/supabase/functions/backfill-quote-images/index.ts` (lines 83-90):
     - Inner try/catch logs but continues loop instead of failing hard
     - Pattern: Per-item error handling can mask batch-level failures
     - All failures are collected in results array and reported, but silent per-quote failures within the loop might hide systematic issues

5. **No Background/Cron Tasks**
   - Only UI-triggered operations with toast feedback
   - No unmonitored scheduled jobs

---

### Verdict

**This codebase is well-maintained for error handling.**

- All errors visible to users and developers
- No swallowed exceptions
- Consistent patterns make maintenance straightforward

**Two issues to consider:**
1. Guard setTimeout redirects with success flags (Upload.tsx)
2. Consider returning early on batch operation failures instead of continuing (backfill function)

Both are **low-risk** in practice since UX provides feedback, but best-practice improvements.</result>

## Audit Report: Error Handling in ~/apps/everything-claude-code/

### Status
**Mixed**: Repository contains both executable code and documentation. Error handling patterns show awareness of issues but with some risk areas.

---

### Critical Findings

**1. Background observer processes with suppressed stderr (CRITICAL)**
- **Files**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (lines 349, 362)
- **Pattern**: `nohup "${SKILL_ROOT}/agents/start-observer.sh" start >/dev/null 2>&1 &`
- **Issue**: Background observer daemon startup failures go completely silent. If the observer fails to start, no diagnostic output is available. Observer log file checking only occurs after 2-second sleep in start-observer.sh (line 211), but failures in the foreground startup script can still silently exit.
- **Severity**: **CRITICAL** — Background observer tasks are automation that runs unattended; failures undetected by users.

**2. Background Claude analysis task without error propagation (CRITICAL)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/agents/observer-loop.sh` (lines 121-142)
- **Pattern**: `timeout_seconds... claude --model haiku... < "$prompt_file" >> "$LOG_FILE" 2>&1 &` followed by `wait "$claude_pid"` 
- **Issue**: Claude process runs in background; exit code is captured but logged silently (line 141: `echo "[$(date)] Claude analysis failed (exit $exit_code)" >> "$LOG_FILE"`). If analysis fails, the loop continues without user notification. Observations file is archived regardless of success (line 147: `mv... 2>/dev/null || true`).
- **Severity**: **CRITICAL** — Pattern analysis failures silently swallowed; user never knows insights failed to generate.

**3. Observer startup with ignored shell errors (CRITICAL)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/agents/observer-loop.sh` (line 8)
- **Pattern**: `set +e` at the top of background observer loop
- **Issue**: `set +e` disables error checking for the entire background process. The comment (line 19) explains it's intentional to prevent claude CLI failures from killing the loop, but this also swallows errors in cleanup and setup. Line 182 has `|| echo "[$(date)] Warning: instinct prune failed (non-fatal)" >> "$LOG_FILE"` but many other commands have no fallback.
- **Severity**: **CRITICAL** — Background automation explicitly ignores errors.

**4. Unmonitored background observer with silent file operations (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (lines 149-154, 231-238, 349-350)
- **Pattern**: `find... -delete 2>/dev/null || true`, `mv... 2>/dev/null || true`, `rm -f... 2>/dev/null || true`
- **Issue**: Observation file archival, observation writes, and purge operations suppress all errors. If disk is full or permissions fail, no alert. Line 350: `nohup... start >/dev/null 2>&1 &` starts observer with no output capture.
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Silent data loss/archival failures.

**5. Subprocess calls without error checking (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/scripts/instinct-cli.py` (lines 140-147, 339-346)
- **Pattern**: `subprocess.run(...capture_output=True)` → check `returncode` but stderr ignored if non-zero
- **Issue**: Git operations fail silently; errors are only logged if detection succeeds. Line 146-147: `except FileNotFoundError: pass` (bare except with pass).
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Git operations can fail silently.

**6. Find with -delete and swallowed errors (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (line 152)
- **Pattern**: `find "${PROJECT_DIR}" -name "observations-*.jsonl" -mtime +30 -delete 2>/dev/null || true`
- **Issue**: File deletion suppresses all errors. If delete fails (permissions, filesystem issues), observation archive cleanup silently fails.
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Silent file operation failures.

---

### Important Findings

**7. Multiple `|| true` fallbacks without logging (IMPORTANT)**
- **Files**: Multiple shell scripts (observer-loop.sh, observe.sh, start-observer.sh, session-guardian.sh)
- **Count**: 43+ instances of `|| true`
- **Pattern**: `command || true` with no fallback action logged
- **Examples**:
  - `kill "$pid" 2>/dev/null || true` (lines 130, 137, 152, 405 in observe.sh) — fails silently
  - `mv... 2>/dev/null || true` (line 147, 237 in observe.sh) — archival failure not logged
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Silences failures that may indicate disk/permission issues.

**8. `2>/dev/null` without fallback (IMPORTANT)**
- **Files**: `observer-loop.sh`, `observe.sh`, `start-observer.sh`, `session-guardian.sh`
- **Count**: 20+ instances
- **Pattern**: `command 2>/dev/null` with no fallback or error logged
- **Examples**:
  - `kill -0 "$pid" 2>/dev/null` (line 128) — can't distinguish "process not running" from "kill failed"
  - `cat "$pid_file" 2>/dev/null` (lines 292-298 in observe.sh) — missing PID file not distinguished from read error
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Diagnostic information lost; can't distinguish missing files from permission errors.

**9. PID file validation insufficient (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (lines 294-306)
- **Issue**: PID files are read and validated with regex, but if `cat` fails, error is silently ignored. Race conditions possible if PID file is deleted between check and read.
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Can signal wrong PID or stale zombie.

---

### Low-Risk Patterns (Acceptable)

**10. Intentional error suppression with clear rationale**
- **Files**: `scripts/codex-git-hooks/pre-commit` (line 38: `rg... 2>/dev/null`), `session-guardian.sh` (line 114: `2>/dev/null || true`)
- **Issue**: These are properly documented (comments explain why stderr is suppressed) and fall back to safe defaults.
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Acceptable trade-off.

**11. Tempfile cleanup with fallback**
- **Files**: `save-results.sh` (line 44), `scan-rules.sh` (line 28), `scan-skills.sh`
- **Pattern**: `trap 'rm -f "$tmp"' EXIT`
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Proper cleanup with trap handlers.

**12. Dry-run mode with explicit logging**
- **File**: `sync-ecc-to-codex.sh` (lines 44-52)
- **Pattern**: All operations logged/echoed, failures show up in output
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Good practice.

---

### Summary Table

| Category | Count | Severity | Actionable |
|----------|-------|----------|-----------|
| Unattended background tasks with suppressed errors | 4 | CRITICAL | Yes: Add logging to nohup invocations |
| Subprocess failures silently logged only | 2 | CRITICAL | Yes: Add stderr capture and alerting |
| Explicit error suppression (`set +e`) | 1 | CRITICAL | Yes: Narrow scope of `set +e` |
| File operations without diagnostics (`2>/dev/null`) | 20+ | IMPORTANT | Partial: Some acceptable, others need logging |
| `\|\| true` without logging | 43+ | IMPORTANT | Partial: Some acceptable, others need fallback |

---

### Recommendations

1. **Observer startup**: Replace `nohup ... >/dev/null 2>&1` with logging to file and stderr capture
2. **Claude analysis failures**: Add user-facing notification when analysis fails (not just logs)
3. **Narrow `set +e`**: Only disable errexit for specific commands that need it, not entire script
4. **File operations**: Log failures for archival, purge, and deletion operations
5. **PID file validation**: Add atomicity check or adopt a lock file instead</result>

<summary>Agent "Audit desktop-organizer" completed</summary>
<result>## Audit Report: desktop-organizer

**Summary:** No critical error-swallowing patterns detected. Code is well-structured with proper error handling.

---

### Findings

| Issue | Severity | Location | Details |
|-------|----------|----------|---------|
| **Subprocess calls with silenced errors** | IMPORTANT | `organizer.py:13-16, 26-28` | `subprocess.run()` calls with `capture_output=True` but no error checking on `returncode`. The `pgrep` wait loop and `say` command could fail silently. |
| **PDF thumbnail fallback** | IMPORTANT | `analyzer.py:26-40` | `qlmanage` subprocess call ignores errors; if generation fails, fallback logic tries to find PNG but doesn't validate success before using it. |
| **HEIC conversion without error check** | IMPORTANT | `analyzer.py:16-23` | `sips` conversion to PNG doesn't check return code; if it fails, empty/invalid PNG is returned downstream. |
| **JSON parse graceful fallback** | LOW | `analyzer.py:205-212` | Bare `except json.JSONDecodeError` with fallback (acceptable—intentional defensive parse). |
| **OSError exception handling** | LOW | `watcher.py:52-62` | Catches `OSError` explicitly in `_wait_for_settle()` but returns `False` rather than re-raising (acceptable—intentional timeout logic). |

---

### Root Causes

1. **subprocess.run() with capture_output=True** (lines 13, 26, 19, 29)
   - No `check=True` parameter
   - No post-call `returncode` validation
   - Failures are silently ignored

2. **No temp file cleanup on subprocess failure** (analyzer.py)
   - `_convert_heic_to_png()` and `_thumbnail_pdf()` don't validate the subprocess succeeded before returning temp paths
   - Dead/empty temp files may accumulate if conversions fail

3. **No background task/cron monitoring**
   - No `.plist`, launchd, or cron config found
   - Not currently daemonized (watchdog in foreground)

---

### Recommendations

- Add `check=True` to `subprocess.run()` calls and let exceptions propagate, OR validate `result.returncode == 0` and log/handle failures
- Validate temp files exist and have content before returning from conversion functions
- If this becomes a background daemon, add logging and error reporting (currently just silent failures via `capture_output=True`)</result>

### Status

- **Files**: `scripts/codex-git-hooks/pre-commit` (line 38: `rg... 2>/dev/null`), `session-guardian.sh` (line 114: `2>/dev/null || true`)
- **Issue**: These are properly documented (comments explain why stderr is suppressed) and fall back to safe defaults.
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Acceptable trade-off.

**11. Tempfile cleanup with fallback**
- **Files**: `save-results.sh` (line 44), `scan-rules.sh` (line 28), `scan-skills.sh`
- **Pattern**: `trap 'rm -f "$tmp"' EXIT`
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Proper cleanup with trap handlers.

**12. Dry-run mode with explicit logging**
- **File**: `sync-ecc-to-codex.sh` (lines 44-52)
- **Pattern**: All operations logged/echoed, failures show up in output
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Good practice.

---

### Summary Table

| Category | Count | Severity | Actionable |
|----------|-------|----------|-----------|
| Unattended background tasks with suppressed errors | 4 | CRITICAL | Yes: Add logging to nohup invocations |
| Subprocess failures silently logged only | 2 | CRITICAL | Yes: Add stderr capture and alerting |
| Explicit error suppression (`set +e`) | 1 | CRITICAL | Yes: Narrow scope of `set +e` |
| File operations without diagnostics (`2>/dev/null`) | 20+ | IMPORTANT | Partial: Some acceptable, others need logging |
| `\|\| true` without logging | 43+ | IMPORTANT | Partial: Some acceptable, others need fallback |

---

### Recommendations

1. **Observer startup**: Replace `nohup ... >/dev/null 2>&1` with logging to file and stderr capture
2. **Claude analysis failures**: Add user-facing notification when analysis fails (not just logs)
3. **Narrow `set +e`**: Only disable errexit for specific commands that need it, not entire script
4. **File operations**: Log failures for archival, purge, and deletion operations
5. **PID file validation**: Add atomicity check or adopt a lock file instead</result>

## Audit Report: Error Handling in ~/apps/everything-claude-code/

### Status
**Mixed**: Repository contains both executable code and documentation. Error handling patterns show awareness of issues but with some risk areas.

---

### Critical Findings

**1. Background observer processes with suppressed stderr (CRITICAL)**
- **Files**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (lines 349, 362)
- **Pattern**: `nohup "${SKILL_ROOT}/agents/start-observer.sh" start >/dev/null 2>&1 &`
- **Issue**: Background observer daemon startup failures go completely silent. If the observer fails to start, no diagnostic output is available. Observer log file checking only occurs after 2-second sleep in start-observer.sh (line 211), but failures in the foreground startup script can still silently exit.
- **Severity**: **CRITICAL** — Background observer tasks are automation that runs unattended; failures undetected by users.

**2. Background Claude analysis task without error propagation (CRITICAL)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/agents/observer-loop.sh` (lines 121-142)
- **Pattern**: `timeout_seconds... claude --model haiku... < "$prompt_file" >> "$LOG_FILE" 2>&1 &` followed by `wait "$claude_pid"` 
- **Issue**: Claude process runs in background; exit code is captured but logged silently (line 141: `echo "[$(date)] Claude analysis failed (exit $exit_code)" >> "$LOG_FILE"`). If analysis fails, the loop continues without user notification. Observations file is archived regardless of success (line 147: `mv... 2>/dev/null || true`).
- **Severity**: **CRITICAL** — Pattern analysis failures silently swallowed; user never knows insights failed to generate.

**3. Observer startup with ignored shell errors (CRITICAL)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/agents/observer-loop.sh` (line 8)
- **Pattern**: `set +e` at the top of background observer loop
- **Issue**: `set +e` disables error checking for the entire background process. The comment (line 19) explains it's intentional to prevent claude CLI failures from killing the loop, but this also swallows errors in cleanup and setup. Line 182 has `|| echo "[$(date)] Warning: instinct prune failed (non-fatal)" >> "$LOG_FILE"` but many other commands have no fallback.
- **Severity**: **CRITICAL** — Background automation explicitly ignores errors.

**4. Unmonitored background observer with silent file operations (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (lines 149-154, 231-238, 349-350)
- **Pattern**: `find... -delete 2>/dev/null || true`, `mv... 2>/dev/null || true`, `rm -f... 2>/dev/null || true`
- **Issue**: Observation file archival, observation writes, and purge operations suppress all errors. If disk is full or permissions fail, no alert. Line 350: `nohup... start >/dev/null 2>&1 &` starts observer with no output capture.
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Silent data loss/archival failures.

**5. Subprocess calls without error checking (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/scripts/instinct-cli.py` (lines 140-147, 339-346)
- **Pattern**: `subprocess.run(...capture_output=True)` → check `returncode` but stderr ignored if non-zero
- **Issue**: Git operations fail silently; errors are only logged if detection succeeds. Line 146-147: `except FileNotFoundError: pass` (bare except with pass).
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Git operations can fail silently.

**6. Find with -delete and swallowed errors (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (line 152)
- **Pattern**: `find "${PROJECT_DIR}" -name "observations-*.jsonl" -mtime +30 -delete 2>/dev/null || true`
- **Issue**: File deletion suppresses all errors. If delete fails (permissions, filesystem issues), observation archive cleanup silently fails.
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Silent file operation failures.

---

### Important Findings

**7. Multiple `|| true` fallbacks without logging (IMPORTANT)**
- **Files**: Multiple shell scripts (observer-loop.sh, observe.sh, start-observer.sh, session-guardian.sh)
- **Count**: 43+ instances of `|| true`
- **Pattern**: `command || true` with no fallback action logged
- **Examples**:
  - `kill "$pid" 2>/dev/null || true` (lines 130, 137, 152, 405 in observe.sh) — fails silently
  - `mv... 2>/dev/null || true` (line 147, 237 in observe.sh) — archival failure not logged
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Silences failures that may indicate disk/permission issues.

**8. `2>/dev/null` without fallback (IMPORTANT)**
- **Files**: `observer-loop.sh`, `observe.sh`, `start-observer.sh`, `session-guardian.sh`
- **Count**: 20+ instances
- **Pattern**: `command 2>/dev/null` with no fallback or error logged
- **Examples**:
  - `kill -0 "$pid" 2>/dev/null` (line 128) — can't distinguish "process not running" from "kill failed"
  - `cat "$pid_file" 2>/dev/null` (lines 292-298 in observe.sh) — missing PID file not distinguished from read error
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Diagnostic information lost; can't distinguish missing files from permission errors.

**9. PID file validation insufficient (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (lines 294-306)
- **Issue**: PID files are read and validated with regex, but if `cat` fails, error is silently ignored. Race conditions possible if PID file is deleted between check and read.
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Can signal wrong PID or stale zombie.

---

### Low-Risk Patterns (Acceptable)

**10. Intentional error suppression with clear rationale**
- **Files**: `scripts/codex-git-hooks/pre-commit` (line 38: `rg... 2>/dev/null`), `session-guardian.sh` (line 114: `2>/dev/null || true`)
- **Issue**: These are properly documented (comments explain why stderr is suppressed) and fall back to safe defaults.
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Acceptable trade-off.

**11. Tempfile cleanup with fallback**
- **Files**: `save-results.sh` (line 44), `scan-rules.sh` (line 28), `scan-skills.sh`
- **Pattern**: `trap 'rm -f "$tmp"' EXIT`
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Proper cleanup with trap handlers.

**12. Dry-run mode with explicit logging**
- **File**: `sync-ecc-to-codex.sh` (lines 44-52)
- **Pattern**: All operations logged/echoed, failures show up in output
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Good practice.

---

### Summary Table

| Category | Count | Severity | Actionable |
|----------|-------|----------|-----------|
| Unattended background tasks with suppressed errors | 4 | CRITICAL | Yes: Add logging to nohup invocations |
| Subprocess failures silently logged only | 2 | CRITICAL | Yes: Add stderr capture and alerting |
| Explicit error suppression (`set +e`) | 1 | CRITICAL | Yes: Narrow scope of `set +e` |
| File operations without diagnostics (`2>/dev/null`) | 20+ | IMPORTANT | Partial: Some acceptable, others need logging |
| `\|\| true` without logging | 43+ | IMPORTANT | Partial: Some acceptable, others need fallback |

---

### Recommendations

1. **Observer startup**: Replace `nohup ... >/dev/null 2>&1` with logging to file and stderr capture
2. **Claude analysis failures**: Add user-facing notification when analysis fails (not just logs)
3. **Narrow `set +e`**: Only disable errexit for specific commands that need it, not entire script
4. **File operations**: Log failures for archival, purge, and deletion operations
5. **PID file validation**: Add atomicity check or adopt a lock file instead</result>

---

## Audit Report: ~/apps/entrepreneur-quotes/

**Project Type:** Executable (React/TypeScript SPA with Supabase backend & Edge Functions)

**Critical Findings: 0 | Important: 2 | Low: 0**

### Summary

This is a **production React application** with a Supabase backend. All error handling follows a **consistent pattern**: errors are caught, logged to console, and user feedback is provided via toast notifications. No swallowed errors, no dangerous shell patterns, no bare except blocks found.

---

### Key Findings

1. **Error Handling Pattern (Good)**
   - All 40+ catch blocks include:
     - `console.error()` for debugging
     - `toast.error()` or `toast.success()` for user feedback
     - `finally` blocks to reset UI state
   - Consistent approach across files: `/src/pages/`, `/src/components/`, `/supabase/functions/`

2. **No Dangerous Patterns Found**
   - ❌ No `; true` or `|| true` (shell suppression)
   - ❌ No `2>/dev/null` without fallback
   - ❌ No bare `except: pass` blocks (Python-style)
   - ❌ No `catch { }` empty blocks
   - ❌ No subprocess calls with ignored errors

3. **setTimeout Unguarded Redirects** — **IMPORTANT**
   - `/src/pages/Upload.tsx` (lines 320 & 671): Redirects fire regardless of success
     ```
     setTimeout(() => { 
       navigate(`/quote/${quote.id}`); // quote.id may be undefined if save fails
     }, 500);
     ```
   - `/src/pages/ResetPassword.tsx` (line 51): Redirects on success but error handling is separate
   - Risk: If the quote save fails but catch block doesn't return, redirect happens to invalid URL

4. **Nested Catch with Inline Error Handling** — **IMPORTANT**
   - `/supabase/functions/backfill-quote-images/index.ts` (lines 83-90):
     - Inner try/catch logs but continues loop instead of failing hard
     - Pattern: Per-item error handling can mask batch-level failures
     - All failures are collected in results array and reported, but silent per-quote failures within the loop might hide systematic issues

5. **No Background/Cron Tasks**
   - Only UI-triggered operations with toast feedback
   - No unmonitored scheduled jobs

---

### Verdict

**This codebase is well-maintained for error handling.**

- All errors visible to users and developers
- No swallowed exceptions
- Consistent patterns make maintenance straightforward

**Two issues to consider:**
1. Guard setTimeout redirects with success flags (Upload.tsx)
2. Consider returning early on batch operation failures instead of continuing (backfill function)

Both are **low-risk** in practice since UX provides feedback, but best-practice improvements.</result>

## Audit Report: ~/apps/entrepreneur-quotes/

**Project Type:** Executable (React/TypeScript SPA with Supabase backend & Edge Functions)

**Critical Findings: 0 | Important: 2 | Low: 0**

### Summary

This is a **production React application** with a Supabase backend. All error handling follows a **consistent pattern**: errors are caught, logged to console, and user feedback is provided via toast notifications. No swallowed errors, no dangerous shell patterns, no bare except blocks found.

---

### Key Findings

1. **Error Handling Pattern (Good)**
   - All 40+ catch blocks include:
     - `console.error()` for debugging
     - `toast.error()` or `toast.success()` for user feedback
     - `finally` blocks to reset UI state
   - Consistent approach across files: `/src/pages/`, `/src/components/`, `/supabase/functions/`

2. **No Dangerous Patterns Found**
   - ❌ No `; true` or `|| true` (shell suppression)
   - ❌ No `2>/dev/null` without fallback
   - ❌ No bare `except: pass` blocks (Python-style)
   - ❌ No `catch { }` empty blocks
   - ❌ No subprocess calls with ignored errors

3. **setTimeout Unguarded Redirects** — **IMPORTANT**
   - `/src/pages/Upload.tsx` (lines 320 & 671): Redirects fire regardless of success
     ```
     setTimeout(() => { 
       navigate(`/quote/${quote.id}`); // quote.id may be undefined if save fails
     }, 500);
     ```
   - `/src/pages/ResetPassword.tsx` (line 51): Redirects on success but error handling is separate
   - Risk: If the quote save fails but catch block doesn't return, redirect happens to invalid URL

4. **Nested Catch with Inline Error Handling** — **IMPORTANT**
   - `/supabase/functions/backfill-quote-images/index.ts` (lines 83-90):
     - Inner try/catch logs but continues loop instead of failing hard
     - Pattern: Per-item error handling can mask batch-level failures
     - All failures are collected in results array and reported, but silent per-quote failures within the loop might hide systematic issues

5. **No Background/Cron Tasks**
   - Only UI-triggered operations with toast feedback
   - No unmonitored scheduled jobs

---

### Verdict

**This codebase is well-maintained for error handling.**

- All errors visible to users and developers
- No swallowed exceptions
- Consistent patterns make maintenance straightforward

**Two issues to consider:**
1. Guard setTimeout redirects with success flags (Upload.tsx)
2. Consider returning early on batch operation failures instead of continuing (backfill function)

Both are **low-risk** in practice since UX provides feedback, but best-practice improvements.</result>

## Audit Report: Error Handling in ~/apps/everything-claude-code/

### Status
**Mixed**: Repository contains both executable code and documentation. Error handling patterns show awareness of issues but with some risk areas.

---

### Critical Findings

**1. Background observer processes with suppressed stderr (CRITICAL)**
- **Files**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (lines 349, 362)
- **Pattern**: `nohup "${SKILL_ROOT}/agents/start-observer.sh" start >/dev/null 2>&1 &`
- **Issue**: Background observer daemon startup failures go completely silent. If the observer fails to start, no diagnostic output is available. Observer log file checking only occurs after 2-second sleep in start-observer.sh (line 211), but failures in the foreground startup script can still silently exit.
- **Severity**: **CRITICAL** — Background observer tasks are automation that runs unattended; failures undetected by users.

**2. Background Claude analysis task without error propagation (CRITICAL)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/agents/observer-loop.sh` (lines 121-142)
- **Pattern**: `timeout_seconds... claude --model haiku... < "$prompt_file" >> "$LOG_FILE" 2>&1 &` followed by `wait "$claude_pid"` 
- **Issue**: Claude process runs in background; exit code is captured but logged silently (line 141: `echo "[$(date)] Claude analysis failed (exit $exit_code)" >> "$LOG_FILE"`). If analysis fails, the loop continues without user notification. Observations file is archived regardless of success (line 147: `mv... 2>/dev/null || true`).
- **Severity**: **CRITICAL** — Pattern analysis failures silently swallowed; user never knows insights failed to generate.

**3. Observer startup with ignored shell errors (CRITICAL)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/agents/observer-loop.sh` (line 8)
- **Pattern**: `set +e` at the top of background observer loop
- **Issue**: `set +e` disables error checking for the entire background process. The comment (line 19) explains it's intentional to prevent claude CLI failures from killing the loop, but this also swallows errors in cleanup and setup. Line 182 has `|| echo "[$(date)] Warning: instinct prune failed (non-fatal)" >> "$LOG_FILE"` but many other commands have no fallback.
- **Severity**: **CRITICAL** — Background automation explicitly ignores errors.

**4. Unmonitored background observer with silent file operations (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (lines 149-154, 231-238, 349-350)
- **Pattern**: `find... -delete 2>/dev/null || true`, `mv... 2>/dev/null || true`, `rm -f... 2>/dev/null || true`
- **Issue**: Observation file archival, observation writes, and purge operations suppress all errors. If disk is full or permissions fail, no alert. Line 350: `nohup... start >/dev/null 2>&1 &` starts observer with no output capture.
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Silent data loss/archival failures.

**5. Subprocess calls without error checking (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/scripts/instinct-cli.py` (lines 140-147, 339-346)
- **Pattern**: `subprocess.run(...capture_output=True)` → check `returncode` but stderr ignored if non-zero
- **Issue**: Git operations fail silently; errors are only logged if detection succeeds. Line 146-147: `except FileNotFoundError: pass` (bare except with pass).
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Git operations can fail silently.

**6. Find with -delete and swallowed errors (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (line 152)
- **Pattern**: `find "${PROJECT_DIR}" -name "observations-*.jsonl" -mtime +30 -delete 2>/dev/null || true`
- **Issue**: File deletion suppresses all errors. If delete fails (permissions, filesystem issues), observation archive cleanup silently fails.
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Silent file operation failures.

---

### Important Findings

**7. Multiple `|| true` fallbacks without logging (IMPORTANT)**
- **Files**: Multiple shell scripts (observer-loop.sh, observe.sh, start-observer.sh, session-guardian.sh)
- **Count**: 43+ instances of `|| true`
- **Pattern**: `command || true` with no fallback action logged
- **Examples**:
  - `kill "$pid" 2>/dev/null || true` (lines 130, 137, 152, 405 in observe.sh) — fails silently
  - `mv... 2>/dev/null || true` (line 147, 237 in observe.sh) — archival failure not logged
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Silences failures that may indicate disk/permission issues.

**8. `2>/dev/null` without fallback (IMPORTANT)**
- **Files**: `observer-loop.sh`, `observe.sh`, `start-observer.sh`, `session-guardian.sh`
- **Count**: 20+ instances
- **Pattern**: `command 2>/dev/null` with no fallback or error logged
- **Examples**:
  - `kill -0 "$pid" 2>/dev/null` (line 128) — can't distinguish "process not running" from "kill failed"
  - `cat "$pid_file" 2>/dev/null` (lines 292-298 in observe.sh) — missing PID file not distinguished from read error
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Diagnostic information lost; can't distinguish missing files from permission errors.

**9. PID file validation insufficient (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (lines 294-306)
- **Issue**: PID files are read and validated with regex, but if `cat` fails, error is silently ignored. Race conditions possible if PID file is deleted between check and read.
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Can signal wrong PID or stale zombie.

---

### Low-Risk Patterns (Acceptable)

**10. Intentional error suppression with clear rationale**
- **Files**: `scripts/codex-git-hooks/pre-commit` (line 38: `rg... 2>/dev/null`), `session-guardian.sh` (line 114: `2>/dev/null || true`)
- **Issue**: These are properly documented (comments explain why stderr is suppressed) and fall back to safe defaults.
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Acceptable trade-off.

**11. Tempfile cleanup with fallback**
- **Files**: `save-results.sh` (line 44), `scan-rules.sh` (line 28), `scan-skills.sh`
- **Pattern**: `trap 'rm -f "$tmp"' EXIT`
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Proper cleanup with trap handlers.

**12. Dry-run mode with explicit logging**
- **File**: `sync-ecc-to-codex.sh` (lines 44-52)
- **Pattern**: All operations logged/echoed, failures show up in output
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Good practice.

---

### Summary Table

| Category | Count | Severity | Actionable |
|----------|-------|----------|-----------|
| Unattended background tasks with suppressed errors | 4 | CRITICAL | Yes: Add logging to nohup invocations |
| Subprocess failures silently logged only | 2 | CRITICAL | Yes: Add stderr capture and alerting |
| Explicit error suppression (`set +e`) | 1 | CRITICAL | Yes: Narrow scope of `set +e` |
| File operations without diagnostics (`2>/dev/null`) | 20+ | IMPORTANT | Partial: Some acceptable, others need logging |
| `\|\| true` without logging | 43+ | IMPORTANT | Partial: Some acceptable, others need fallback |

---

### Recommendations

1. **Observer startup**: Replace `nohup ... >/dev/null 2>&1` with logging to file and stderr capture
2. **Claude analysis failures**: Add user-facing notification when analysis fails (not just logs)
3. **Narrow `set +e`**: Only disable errexit for specific commands that need it, not entire script
4. **File operations**: Log failures for archival, purge, and deletion operations
5. **PID file validation**: Add atomicity check or adopt a lock file instead</result>

## AUDIT REPORT: ~/apps/entrepreneurquotes/

**PROJECT TYPE:** Frontend React/TypeScript app + Supabase serverless functions. No shell scripts or cron jobs.

**SEVERITY SUMMARY: LOW**

### Findings

**No Critical Issues Found:**
- No `; true` or `|| true` patterns (shell suppression)
- No `2>/dev/null` stderr redirection
- No bare `except:` or `except: pass` blocks (Python)
- No empty `catch() {}` blocks
- No subprocess calls with ignored errors
- No cron/background task files

### Error Handling Assessment

**Strong Points:**
1. **Supabase Functions** - All 5 functions have explicit try-catch with proper error responses:
   - `/download-image`: Timeout handling, status checks, detailed error messages
   - `/analyze-quote-meaning`: API error differentiation (429, 402), proper error mapping
   - `/analyze-quote-text`: Same robust pattern as above
   - `/analyze-quote`: Comprehensive error handling with validation
   - `/backfill-quote-images`: Per-quote error isolation in loop, results tracking

2. **React Components** - All have error handling:
   - `BackfillImages.tsx`: Try-catch with user feedback via toast
   - `BackfillCategories.tsx`: Per-item error capture with status tracking
   - `Upload.tsx`: Comprehensive validation and error states
   - All errors logged to console + user-facing messages

3. **API Calls**: Consistent pattern of checking response.ok and status codes before consuming data

### Minor Observations (Not Issues)

- Some `console.error()` calls without additional telemetry, but this is acceptable for a frontend app
- Supabase functions use generic "Unknown error" fallback, but this is safely handled
- No unhandled promise rejections observed

**VERDICT:** Project demonstrates good error-handling discipline. No swallowed errors or hidden failures detected. Safe for production.</result>

## Audit Report: ~/apps/entrepreneur-quotes/

**Project Type:** Executable (React/TypeScript SPA with Supabase backend & Edge Functions)

**Critical Findings: 0 | Important: 2 | Low: 0**

### Summary

This is a **production React application** with a Supabase backend. All error handling follows a **consistent pattern**: errors are caught, logged to console, and user feedback is provided via toast notifications. No swallowed errors, no dangerous shell patterns, no bare except blocks found.

---

### Key Findings

1. **Error Handling Pattern (Good)**
   - All 40+ catch blocks include:
     - `console.error()` for debugging
     - `toast.error()` or `toast.success()` for user feedback
     - `finally` blocks to reset UI state
   - Consistent approach across files: `/src/pages/`, `/src/components/`, `/supabase/functions/`

2. **No Dangerous Patterns Found**
   - ❌ No `; true` or `|| true` (shell suppression)
   - ❌ No `2>/dev/null` without fallback
   - ❌ No bare `except: pass` blocks (Python-style)
   - ❌ No `catch { }` empty blocks
   - ❌ No subprocess calls with ignored errors

3. **setTimeout Unguarded Redirects** — **IMPORTANT**
   - `/src/pages/Upload.tsx` (lines 320 & 671): Redirects fire regardless of success
     ```
     setTimeout(() => { 
       navigate(`/quote/${quote.id}`); // quote.id may be undefined if save fails
     }, 500);
     ```
   - `/src/pages/ResetPassword.tsx` (line 51): Redirects on success but error handling is separate
   - Risk: If the quote save fails but catch block doesn't return, redirect happens to invalid URL

4. **Nested Catch with Inline Error Handling** — **IMPORTANT**
   - `/supabase/functions/backfill-quote-images/index.ts` (lines 83-90):
     - Inner try/catch logs but continues loop instead of failing hard
     - Pattern: Per-item error handling can mask batch-level failures
     - All failures are collected in results array and reported, but silent per-quote failures within the loop might hide systematic issues

5. **No Background/Cron Tasks**
   - Only UI-triggered operations with toast feedback
   - No unmonitored scheduled jobs

---

### Verdict

**This codebase is well-maintained for error handling.**

- All errors visible to users and developers
- No swallowed exceptions
- Consistent patterns make maintenance straightforward

**Two issues to consider:**
1. Guard setTimeout redirects with success flags (Upload.tsx)
2. Consider returning early on batch operation failures instead of continuing (backfill function)

Both are **low-risk** in practice since UX provides feedback, but best-practice improvements.</result>

## Audit Report: Error Handling in ~/apps/everything-claude-code/

### Status
**Mixed**: Repository contains both executable code and documentation. Error handling patterns show awareness of issues but with some risk areas.

---

### Critical Findings

**1. Background observer processes with suppressed stderr (CRITICAL)**
- **Files**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (lines 349, 362)
- **Pattern**: `nohup "${SKILL_ROOT}/agents/start-observer.sh" start >/dev/null 2>&1 &`
- **Issue**: Background observer daemon startup failures go completely silent. If the observer fails to start, no diagnostic output is available. Observer log file checking only occurs after 2-second sleep in start-observer.sh (line 211), but failures in the foreground startup script can still silently exit.
- **Severity**: **CRITICAL** — Background observer tasks are automation that runs unattended; failures undetected by users.

**2. Background Claude analysis task without error propagation (CRITICAL)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/agents/observer-loop.sh` (lines 121-142)
- **Pattern**: `timeout_seconds... claude --model haiku... < "$prompt_file" >> "$LOG_FILE" 2>&1 &` followed by `wait "$claude_pid"` 
- **Issue**: Claude process runs in background; exit code is captured but logged silently (line 141: `echo "[$(date)] Claude analysis failed (exit $exit_code)" >> "$LOG_FILE"`). If analysis fails, the loop continues without user notification. Observations file is archived regardless of success (line 147: `mv... 2>/dev/null || true`).
- **Severity**: **CRITICAL** — Pattern analysis failures silently swallowed; user never knows insights failed to generate.

**3. Observer startup with ignored shell errors (CRITICAL)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/agents/observer-loop.sh` (line 8)
- **Pattern**: `set +e` at the top of background observer loop
- **Issue**: `set +e` disables error checking for the entire background process. The comment (line 19) explains it's intentional to prevent claude CLI failures from killing the loop, but this also swallows errors in cleanup and setup. Line 182 has `|| echo "[$(date)] Warning: instinct prune failed (non-fatal)" >> "$LOG_FILE"` but many other commands have no fallback.
- **Severity**: **CRITICAL** — Background automation explicitly ignores errors.

**4. Unmonitored background observer with silent file operations (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (lines 149-154, 231-238, 349-350)
- **Pattern**: `find... -delete 2>/dev/null || true`, `mv... 2>/dev/null || true`, `rm -f... 2>/dev/null || true`
- **Issue**: Observation file archival, observation writes, and purge operations suppress all errors. If disk is full or permissions fail, no alert. Line 350: `nohup... start >/dev/null 2>&1 &` starts observer with no output capture.
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Silent data loss/archival failures.

**5. Subprocess calls without error checking (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/scripts/instinct-cli.py` (lines 140-147, 339-346)
- **Pattern**: `subprocess.run(...capture_output=True)` → check `returncode` but stderr ignored if non-zero
- **Issue**: Git operations fail silently; errors are only logged if detection succeeds. Line 146-147: `except FileNotFoundError: pass` (bare except with pass).
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Git operations can fail silently.

**6. Find with -delete and swallowed errors (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (line 152)
- **Pattern**: `find "${PROJECT_DIR}" -name "observations-*.jsonl" -mtime +30 -delete 2>/dev/null || true`
- **Issue**: File deletion suppresses all errors. If delete fails (permissions, filesystem issues), observation archive cleanup silently fails.
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Silent file operation failures.

---

### Important Findings

**7. Multiple `|| true` fallbacks without logging (IMPORTANT)**
- **Files**: Multiple shell scripts (observer-loop.sh, observe.sh, start-observer.sh, session-guardian.sh)
- **Count**: 43+ instances of `|| true`
- **Pattern**: `command || true` with no fallback action logged
- **Examples**:
  - `kill "$pid" 2>/dev/null || true` (lines 130, 137, 152, 405 in observe.sh) — fails silently
  - `mv... 2>/dev/null || true` (line 147, 237 in observe.sh) — archival failure not logged
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Silences failures that may indicate disk/permission issues.

**8. `2>/dev/null` without fallback (IMPORTANT)**
- **Files**: `observer-loop.sh`, `observe.sh`, `start-observer.sh`, `session-guardian.sh`
- **Count**: 20+ instances
- **Pattern**: `command 2>/dev/null` with no fallback or error logged
- **Examples**:
  - `kill -0 "$pid" 2>/dev/null` (line 128) — can't distinguish "process not running" from "kill failed"
  - `cat "$pid_file" 2>/dev/null` (lines 292-298 in observe.sh) — missing PID file not distinguished from read error
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Diagnostic information lost; can't distinguish missing files from permission errors.

**9. PID file validation insufficient (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (lines 294-306)
- **Issue**: PID files are read and validated with regex, but if `cat` fails, error is silently ignored. Race conditions possible if PID file is deleted between check and read.
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Can signal wrong PID or stale zombie.

---

### Low-Risk Patterns (Acceptable)

**10. Intentional error suppression with clear rationale**
- **Files**: `scripts/codex-git-hooks/pre-commit` (line 38: `rg... 2>/dev/null`), `session-guardian.sh` (line 114: `2>/dev/null || true`)
- **Issue**: These are properly documented (comments explain why stderr is suppressed) and fall back to safe defaults.
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Acceptable trade-off.

**11. Tempfile cleanup with fallback**
- **Files**: `save-results.sh` (line 44), `scan-rules.sh` (line 28), `scan-skills.sh`
- **Pattern**: `trap 'rm -f "$tmp"' EXIT`
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Proper cleanup with trap handlers.

**12. Dry-run mode with explicit logging**
- **File**: `sync-ecc-to-codex.sh` (lines 44-52)
- **Pattern**: All operations logged/echoed, failures show up in output
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Good practice.

---

### Summary Table

| Category | Count | Severity | Actionable |
|----------|-------|----------|-----------|
| Unattended background tasks with suppressed errors | 4 | CRITICAL | Yes: Add logging to nohup invocations |
| Subprocess failures silently logged only | 2 | CRITICAL | Yes: Add stderr capture and alerting |
| Explicit error suppression (`set +e`) | 1 | CRITICAL | Yes: Narrow scope of `set +e` |
| File operations without diagnostics (`2>/dev/null`) | 20+ | IMPORTANT | Partial: Some acceptable, others need logging |
| `\|\| true` without logging | 43+ | IMPORTANT | Partial: Some acceptable, others need fallback |

---

### Recommendations

1. **Observer startup**: Replace `nohup ... >/dev/null 2>&1` with logging to file and stderr capture
2. **Claude analysis failures**: Add user-facing notification when analysis fails (not just logs)
3. **Narrow `set +e`**: Only disable errexit for specific commands that need it, not entire script
4. **File operations**: Log failures for archival, purge, and deletion operations
5. **PID file validation**: Add atomicity check or adopt a lock file instead</result>

- **Pattern**: `trap 'rm -f "$tmp"' EXIT`
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Proper cleanup with trap handlers.

**12. Dry-run mode with explicit logging**
- **File**: `sync-ecc-to-codex.sh` (lines 44-52)
- **Pattern**: All operations logged/echoed, failures show up in output
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Good practice.

|----------|-------|----------|-----------|
| Unattended background tasks with suppressed errors | 4 | CRITICAL | Yes: Add logging to nohup invocations |
| Subprocess failures silently logged only | 2 | CRITICAL | Yes: Add stderr capture and alerting |
| Explicit error suppression (`set +e`) | 1 | CRITICAL | Yes: Narrow scope of `set +e` |
| File operations without diagnostics (`2>/dev/null`) | 20+ | IMPORTANT | Partial: Some acceptable, others need logging |
| `\|\| true` without logging | 43+ | IMPORTANT | Partial: Some acceptable, others need fallback |

### Recommendations

1. **Observer startup**: Replace `nohup ... >/dev/null 2>&1` with logging to file and stderr capture
2. **Claude analysis failures**: Add user-facing notification when analysis fails (not just logs)
3. **Narrow `set +e`**: Only disable errexit for specific commands that need it, not entire script
4. **File operations**: Log failures for archival, purge, and deletion operations
5. **PID file validation**: Add atomicity check or adopt a lock file instead</result>

## Audit Report: ~/apps/entrepreneur-quotes/

**Project Type:** Executable (React/TypeScript SPA with Supabase backend & Edge Functions)

**Critical Findings: 0 | Important: 2 | Low: 0**

### Summary

This is a **production React application** with a Supabase backend. All error handling follows a **consistent pattern**: errors are caught, logged to console, and user feedback is provided via toast notifications. No swallowed errors, no dangerous shell patterns, no bare except blocks found.

---

### Key Findings

1. **Error Handling Pattern (Good)**
   - All 40+ catch blocks include:
     - `console.error()` for debugging
     - `toast.error()` or `toast.success()` for user feedback
     - `finally` blocks to reset UI state
   - Consistent approach across files: `/src/pages/`, `/src/components/`, `/supabase/functions/`

2. **No Dangerous Patterns Found**
   - ❌ No `; true` or `|| true` (shell suppression)
   - ❌ No `2>/dev/null` without fallback
   - ❌ No bare `except: pass` blocks (Python-style)
   - ❌ No `catch { }` empty blocks
   - ❌ No subprocess calls with ignored errors

3. **setTimeout Unguarded Redirects** — **IMPORTANT**
   - `/src/pages/Upload.tsx` (lines 320 & 671): Redirects fire regardless of success
     ```
     setTimeout(() => { 
       navigate(`/quote/${quote.id}`); // quote.id may be undefined if save fails
     }, 500);
     ```
   - `/src/pages/ResetPassword.tsx` (line 51): Redirects on success but error handling is separate
   - Risk: If the quote save fails but catch block doesn't return, redirect happens to invalid URL

4. **Nested Catch with Inline Error Handling** — **IMPORTANT**
   - `/supabase/functions/backfill-quote-images/index.ts` (lines 83-90):
     - Inner try/catch logs but continues loop instead of failing hard
     - Pattern: Per-item error handling can mask batch-level failures
     - All failures are collected in results array and reported, but silent per-quote failures within the loop might hide systematic issues

5. **No Background/Cron Tasks**
   - Only UI-triggered operations with toast feedback
   - No unmonitored scheduled jobs

---

### Verdict

**This codebase is well-maintained for error handling.**

- All errors visible to users and developers
- No swallowed exceptions
- Consistent patterns make maintenance straightforward

**Two issues to consider:**
1. Guard setTimeout redirects with success flags (Upload.tsx)
2. Consider returning early on batch operation failures instead of continuing (backfill function)

Both are **low-risk** in practice since UX provides feedback, but best-practice improvements.</result>

## Audit Report: Error Handling in ~/apps/everything-claude-code/

### Status
**Mixed**: Repository contains both executable code and documentation. Error handling patterns show awareness of issues but with some risk areas.

---

### Critical Findings

**1. Background observer processes with suppressed stderr (CRITICAL)**
- **Files**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (lines 349, 362)
- **Pattern**: `nohup "${SKILL_ROOT}/agents/start-observer.sh" start >/dev/null 2>&1 &`
- **Issue**: Background observer daemon startup failures go completely silent. If the observer fails to start, no diagnostic output is available. Observer log file checking only occurs after 2-second sleep in start-observer.sh (line 211), but failures in the foreground startup script can still silently exit.
- **Severity**: **CRITICAL** — Background observer tasks are automation that runs unattended; failures undetected by users.

**2. Background Claude analysis task without error propagation (CRITICAL)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/agents/observer-loop.sh` (lines 121-142)
- **Pattern**: `timeout_seconds... claude --model haiku... < "$prompt_file" >> "$LOG_FILE" 2>&1 &` followed by `wait "$claude_pid"` 
- **Issue**: Claude process runs in background; exit code is captured but logged silently (line 141: `echo "[$(date)] Claude analysis failed (exit $exit_code)" >> "$LOG_FILE"`). If analysis fails, the loop continues without user notification. Observations file is archived regardless of success (line 147: `mv... 2>/dev/null || true`).
- **Severity**: **CRITICAL** — Pattern analysis failures silently swallowed; user never knows insights failed to generate.

**3. Observer startup with ignored shell errors (CRITICAL)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/agents/observer-loop.sh` (line 8)
- **Pattern**: `set +e` at the top of background observer loop
- **Issue**: `set +e` disables error checking for the entire background process. The comment (line 19) explains it's intentional to prevent claude CLI failures from killing the loop, but this also swallows errors in cleanup and setup. Line 182 has `|| echo "[$(date)] Warning: instinct prune failed (non-fatal)" >> "$LOG_FILE"` but many other commands have no fallback.
- **Severity**: **CRITICAL** — Background automation explicitly ignores errors.

**4. Unmonitored background observer with silent file operations (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (lines 149-154, 231-238, 349-350)
- **Pattern**: `find... -delete 2>/dev/null || true`, `mv... 2>/dev/null || true`, `rm -f... 2>/dev/null || true`
- **Issue**: Observation file archival, observation writes, and purge operations suppress all errors. If disk is full or permissions fail, no alert. Line 350: `nohup... start >/dev/null 2>&1 &` starts observer with no output capture.
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Silent data loss/archival failures.

**5. Subprocess calls without error checking (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/scripts/instinct-cli.py` (lines 140-147, 339-346)
- **Pattern**: `subprocess.run(...capture_output=True)` → check `returncode` but stderr ignored if non-zero
- **Issue**: Git operations fail silently; errors are only logged if detection succeeds. Line 146-147: `except FileNotFoundError: pass` (bare except with pass).
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Git operations can fail silently.

**6. Find with -delete and swallowed errors (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (line 152)
- **Pattern**: `find "${PROJECT_DIR}" -name "observations-*.jsonl" -mtime +30 -delete 2>/dev/null || true`
- **Issue**: File deletion suppresses all errors. If delete fails (permissions, filesystem issues), observation archive cleanup silently fails.
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Silent file operation failures.

---

### Important Findings

**7. Multiple `|| true` fallbacks without logging (IMPORTANT)**
- **Files**: Multiple shell scripts (observer-loop.sh, observe.sh, start-observer.sh, session-guardian.sh)
- **Count**: 43+ instances of `|| true`
- **Pattern**: `command || true` with no fallback action logged
- **Examples**:
  - `kill "$pid" 2>/dev/null || true` (lines 130, 137, 152, 405 in observe.sh) — fails silently
  - `mv... 2>/dev/null || true` (line 147, 237 in observe.sh) — archival failure not logged
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Silences failures that may indicate disk/permission issues.

**8. `2>/dev/null` without fallback (IMPORTANT)**
- **Files**: `observer-loop.sh`, `observe.sh`, `start-observer.sh`, `session-guardian.sh`
- **Count**: 20+ instances
- **Pattern**: `command 2>/dev/null` with no fallback or error logged
- **Examples**:
  - `kill -0 "$pid" 2>/dev/null` (line 128) — can't distinguish "process not running" from "kill failed"
  - `cat "$pid_file" 2>/dev/null` (lines 292-298 in observe.sh) — missing PID file not distinguished from read error
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Diagnostic information lost; can't distinguish missing files from permission errors.

**9. PID file validation insufficient (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (lines 294-306)
- **Issue**: PID files are read and validated with regex, but if `cat` fails, error is silently ignored. Race conditions possible if PID file is deleted between check and read.
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Can signal wrong PID or stale zombie.

---

### Low-Risk Patterns (Acceptable)

**10. Intentional error suppression with clear rationale**
- **Files**: `scripts/codex-git-hooks/pre-commit` (line 38: `rg... 2>/dev/null`), `session-guardian.sh` (line 114: `2>/dev/null || true`)
- **Issue**: These are properly documented (comments explain why stderr is suppressed) and fall back to safe defaults.
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Acceptable trade-off.

**11. Tempfile cleanup with fallback**
- **Files**: `save-results.sh` (line 44), `scan-rules.sh` (line 28), `scan-skills.sh`
- **Pattern**: `trap 'rm -f "$tmp"' EXIT`
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Proper cleanup with trap handlers.

**12. Dry-run mode with explicit logging**
- **File**: `sync-ecc-to-codex.sh` (lines 44-52)
- **Pattern**: All operations logged/echoed, failures show up in output
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Good practice.

---

### Summary Table

| Category | Count | Severity | Actionable |
|----------|-------|----------|-----------|
| Unattended background tasks with suppressed errors | 4 | CRITICAL | Yes: Add logging to nohup invocations |
| Subprocess failures silently logged only | 2 | CRITICAL | Yes: Add stderr capture and alerting |
| Explicit error suppression (`set +e`) | 1 | CRITICAL | Yes: Narrow scope of `set +e` |
| File operations without diagnostics (`2>/dev/null`) | 20+ | IMPORTANT | Partial: Some acceptable, others need logging |
| `\|\| true` without logging | 43+ | IMPORTANT | Partial: Some acceptable, others need fallback |

---

### Recommendations

1. **Observer startup**: Replace `nohup ... >/dev/null 2>&1` with logging to file and stderr capture
2. **Claude analysis failures**: Add user-facing notification when analysis fails (not just logs)
3. **Narrow `set +e`**: Only disable errexit for specific commands that need it, not entire script
4. **File operations**: Log failures for archival, purge, and deletion operations
5. **PID file validation**: Add atomicity check or adopt a lock file instead</result>

## Audit Report: Error Handling in ~/apps/everything-claude-code/

### Status
**Mixed**: Repository contains both executable code and documentation. Error handling patterns show awareness of issues but with some risk areas.

---

### Critical Findings

**1. Background observer processes with suppressed stderr (CRITICAL)**
- **Files**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (lines 349, 362)
- **Pattern**: `nohup "${SKILL_ROOT}/agents/start-observer.sh" start >/dev/null 2>&1 &`
- **Issue**: Background observer daemon startup failures go completely silent. If the observer fails to start, no diagnostic output is available. Observer log file checking only occurs after 2-second sleep in start-observer.sh (line 211), but failures in the foreground startup script can still silently exit.
- **Severity**: **CRITICAL** — Background observer tasks are automation that runs unattended; failures undetected by users.

**2. Background Claude analysis task without error propagation (CRITICAL)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/agents/observer-loop.sh` (lines 121-142)
- **Pattern**: `timeout_seconds... claude --model haiku... < "$prompt_file" >> "$LOG_FILE" 2>&1 &` followed by `wait "$claude_pid"` 
- **Issue**: Claude process runs in background; exit code is captured but logged silently (line 141: `echo "[$(date)] Claude analysis failed (exit $exit_code)" >> "$LOG_FILE"`). If analysis fails, the loop continues without user notification. Observations file is archived regardless of success (line 147: `mv... 2>/dev/null || true`).
- **Severity**: **CRITICAL** — Pattern analysis failures silently swallowed; user never knows insights failed to generate.

**3. Observer startup with ignored shell errors (CRITICAL)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/agents/observer-loop.sh` (line 8)
- **Pattern**: `set +e` at the top of background observer loop
- **Issue**: `set +e` disables error checking for the entire background process. The comment (line 19) explains it's intentional to prevent claude CLI failures from killing the loop, but this also swallows errors in cleanup and setup. Line 182 has `|| echo "[$(date)] Warning: instinct prune failed (non-fatal)" >> "$LOG_FILE"` but many other commands have no fallback.
- **Severity**: **CRITICAL** — Background automation explicitly ignores errors.

**4. Unmonitored background observer with silent file operations (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (lines 149-154, 231-238, 349-350)
- **Pattern**: `find... -delete 2>/dev/null || true`, `mv... 2>/dev/null || true`, `rm -f... 2>/dev/null || true`
- **Issue**: Observation file archival, observation writes, and purge operations suppress all errors. If disk is full or permissions fail, no alert. Line 350: `nohup... start >/dev/null 2>&1 &` starts observer with no output capture.
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Silent data loss/archival failures.

**5. Subprocess calls without error checking (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/scripts/instinct-cli.py` (lines 140-147, 339-346)
- **Pattern**: `subprocess.run(...capture_output=True)` → check `returncode` but stderr ignored if non-zero
- **Issue**: Git operations fail silently; errors are only logged if detection succeeds. Line 146-147: `except FileNotFoundError: pass` (bare except with pass).
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Git operations can fail silently.

**6. Find with -delete and swallowed errors (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (line 152)
- **Pattern**: `find "${PROJECT_DIR}" -name "observations-*.jsonl" -mtime +30 -delete 2>/dev/null || true`
- **Issue**: File deletion suppresses all errors. If delete fails (permissions, filesystem issues), observation archive cleanup silently fails.
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Silent file operation failures.

---

### Important Findings

**7. Multiple `|| true` fallbacks without logging (IMPORTANT)**
- **Files**: Multiple shell scripts (observer-loop.sh, observe.sh, start-observer.sh, session-guardian.sh)
- **Count**: 43+ instances of `|| true`
- **Pattern**: `command || true` with no fallback action logged
- **Examples**:
  - `kill "$pid" 2>/dev/null || true` (lines 130, 137, 152, 405 in observe.sh) — fails silently
  - `mv... 2>/dev/null || true` (line 147, 237 in observe.sh) — archival failure not logged
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Silences failures that may indicate disk/permission issues.

**8. `2>/dev/null` without fallback (IMPORTANT)**
- **Files**: `observer-loop.sh`, `observe.sh`, `start-observer.sh`, `session-guardian.sh`
- **Count**: 20+ instances
- **Pattern**: `command 2>/dev/null` with no fallback or error logged
- **Examples**:
  - `kill -0 "$pid" 2>/dev/null` (line 128) — can't distinguish "process not running" from "kill failed"
  - `cat "$pid_file" 2>/dev/null` (lines 292-298 in observe.sh) — missing PID file not distinguished from read error
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Diagnostic information lost; can't distinguish missing files from permission errors.

**9. PID file validation insufficient (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (lines 294-306)
- **Issue**: PID files are read and validated with regex, but if `cat` fails, error is silently ignored. Race conditions possible if PID file is deleted between check and read.
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Can signal wrong PID or stale zombie.

---

### Low-Risk Patterns (Acceptable)

**10. Intentional error suppression with clear rationale**
- **Files**: `scripts/codex-git-hooks/pre-commit` (line 38: `rg... 2>/dev/null`), `session-guardian.sh` (line 114: `2>/dev/null || true`)
- **Issue**: These are properly documented (comments explain why stderr is suppressed) and fall back to safe defaults.
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Acceptable trade-off.

**11. Tempfile cleanup with fallback**
- **Files**: `save-results.sh` (line 44), `scan-rules.sh` (line 28), `scan-skills.sh`
- **Pattern**: `trap 'rm -f "$tmp"' EXIT`
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Proper cleanup with trap handlers.

**12. Dry-run mode with explicit logging**
- **File**: `sync-ecc-to-codex.sh` (lines 44-52)
- **Pattern**: All operations logged/echoed, failures show up in output
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Good practice.

---

### Summary Table

| Category | Count | Severity | Actionable |
|----------|-------|----------|-----------|
| Unattended background tasks with suppressed errors | 4 | CRITICAL | Yes: Add logging to nohup invocations |
| Subprocess failures silently logged only | 2 | CRITICAL | Yes: Add stderr capture and alerting |
| Explicit error suppression (`set +e`) | 1 | CRITICAL | Yes: Narrow scope of `set +e` |
| File operations without diagnostics (`2>/dev/null`) | 20+ | IMPORTANT | Partial: Some acceptable, others need logging |
| `\|\| true` without logging | 43+ | IMPORTANT | Partial: Some acceptable, others need fallback |

---

### Recommendations

1. **Observer startup**: Replace `nohup ... >/dev/null 2>&1` with logging to file and stderr capture
2. **Claude analysis failures**: Add user-facing notification when analysis fails (not just logs)
3. **Narrow `set +e`**: Only disable errexit for specific commands that need it, not entire script
4. **File operations**: Log failures for archival, purge, and deletion operations
5. **PID file validation**: Add atomicity check or adopt a lock file instead</result>

---

## Audit Report: ~/apps/entrepreneur-quotes/

**Project Type:** Executable (React/TypeScript SPA with Supabase backend & Edge Functions)

**Critical Findings: 0 | Important: 2 | Low: 0**

### Summary

This is a **production React application** with a Supabase backend. All error handling follows a **consistent pattern**: errors are caught, logged to console, and user feedback is provided via toast notifications. No swallowed errors, no dangerous shell patterns, no bare except blocks found.

---

### Key Findings

1. **Error Handling Pattern (Good)**
   - All 40+ catch blocks include:
     - `console.error()` for debugging
     - `toast.error()` or `toast.success()` for user feedback
     - `finally` blocks to reset UI state
   - Consistent approach across files: `/src/pages/`, `/src/components/`, `/supabase/functions/`

2. **No Dangerous Patterns Found**
   - ❌ No `; true` or `|| true` (shell suppression)
   - ❌ No `2>/dev/null` without fallback
   - ❌ No bare `except: pass` blocks (Python-style)
   - ❌ No `catch { }` empty blocks
   - ❌ No subprocess calls with ignored errors

3. **setTimeout Unguarded Redirects** — **IMPORTANT**
   - `/src/pages/Upload.tsx` (lines 320 & 671): Redirects fire regardless of success
     ```
     setTimeout(() => { 
       navigate(`/quote/${quote.id}`); // quote.id may be undefined if save fails
     }, 500);
     ```
   - `/src/pages/ResetPassword.tsx` (line 51): Redirects on success but error handling is separate
   - Risk: If the quote save fails but catch block doesn't return, redirect happens to invalid URL

4. **Nested Catch with Inline Error Handling** — **IMPORTANT**
   - `/supabase/functions/backfill-quote-images/index.ts` (lines 83-90):
     - Inner try/catch logs but continues loop instead of failing hard
     - Pattern: Per-item error handling can mask batch-level failures
     - All failures are collected in results array and reported, but silent per-quote failures within the loop might hide systematic issues

5. **No Background/Cron Tasks**
   - Only UI-triggered operations with toast feedback
   - No unmonitored scheduled jobs

---

### Verdict

**This codebase is well-maintained for error handling.**

- All errors visible to users and developers
- No swallowed exceptions
- Consistent patterns make maintenance straightforward

**Two issues to consider:**
1. Guard setTimeout redirects with success flags (Upload.tsx)
2. Consider returning early on batch operation failures instead of continuing (backfill function)

Both are **low-risk** in practice since UX provides feedback, but best-practice improvements.</result>

   - **Line 148:** `mv` for archiving observations now logs errors to `$LOG_FILE` with a `[OBSERVER] WARNING` prefix instead of silently swallowing them with `2>/dev/null || true`.

3. `/Users/ojhurst/apps/everything-claude-code/skills/continuous-learning-v2/scripts/instinct-cli.py`
   - **Line 146-148:** The `except (subprocess.TimeoutExpired, FileNotFoundError)` now prints a diagnostic to stderr before the `pass`, so git-not-found situations are not completely silent.

No business logic changed. `set +e` remains in observer-loop.sh. `|| true` on kill commands left untouched.</result>

## Audit Report: ~/apps/entrepreneur-quotes/

**Project Type:** Executable (React/TypeScript SPA with Supabase backend & Edge Functions)

**Critical Findings: 0 | Important: 2 | Low: 0**

### Summary

This is a **production React application** with a Supabase backend. All error handling follows a **consistent pattern**: errors are caught, logged to console, and user feedback is provided via toast notifications. No swallowed errors, no dangerous shell patterns, no bare except blocks found.

---

### Key Findings

1. **Error Handling Pattern (Good)**
   - All 40+ catch blocks include:
     - `console.error()` for debugging
     - `toast.error()` or `toast.success()` for user feedback
     - `finally` blocks to reset UI state
   - Consistent approach across files: `/src/pages/`, `/src/components/`, `/supabase/functions/`

2. **No Dangerous Patterns Found**
   - ❌ No `; true` or `|| true` (shell suppression)
   - ❌ No `2>/dev/null` without fallback
   - ❌ No bare `except: pass` blocks (Python-style)
   - ❌ No `catch { }` empty blocks
   - ❌ No subprocess calls with ignored errors

3. **setTimeout Unguarded Redirects** — **IMPORTANT**
   - `/src/pages/Upload.tsx` (lines 320 & 671): Redirects fire regardless of success
     ```
     setTimeout(() => { 
       navigate(`/quote/${quote.id}`); // quote.id may be undefined if save fails
     }, 500);
     ```
   - `/src/pages/ResetPassword.tsx` (line 51): Redirects on success but error handling is separate
   - Risk: If the quote save fails but catch block doesn't return, redirect happens to invalid URL

4. **Nested Catch with Inline Error Handling** — **IMPORTANT**
   - `/supabase/functions/backfill-quote-images/index.ts` (lines 83-90):
     - Inner try/catch logs but continues loop instead of failing hard
     - Pattern: Per-item error handling can mask batch-level failures
     - All failures are collected in results array and reported, but silent per-quote failures within the loop might hide systematic issues

5. **No Background/Cron Tasks**
   - Only UI-triggered operations with toast feedback
   - No unmonitored scheduled jobs

---

### Verdict

**This codebase is well-maintained for error handling.**

- All errors visible to users and developers
- No swallowed exceptions
- Consistent patterns make maintenance straightforward

**Two issues to consider:**
1. Guard setTimeout redirects with success flags (Upload.tsx)
2. Consider returning early on batch operation failures instead of continuing (backfill function)

Both are **low-risk** in practice since UX provides feedback, but best-practice improvements.</result>

## Audit Report: Error Handling in ~/apps/everything-claude-code/

### Status
**Mixed**: Repository contains both executable code and documentation. Error handling patterns show awareness of issues but with some risk areas.

---

### Critical Findings

**1. Background observer processes with suppressed stderr (CRITICAL)**
- **Files**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (lines 349, 362)
- **Pattern**: `nohup "${SKILL_ROOT}/agents/start-observer.sh" start >/dev/null 2>&1 &`
- **Issue**: Background observer daemon startup failures go completely silent. If the observer fails to start, no diagnostic output is available. Observer log file checking only occurs after 2-second sleep in start-observer.sh (line 211), but failures in the foreground startup script can still silently exit.
- **Severity**: **CRITICAL** — Background observer tasks are automation that runs unattended; failures undetected by users.

**2. Background Claude analysis task without error propagation (CRITICAL)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/agents/observer-loop.sh` (lines 121-142)
- **Pattern**: `timeout_seconds... claude --model haiku... < "$prompt_file" >> "$LOG_FILE" 2>&1 &` followed by `wait "$claude_pid"` 
- **Issue**: Claude process runs in background; exit code is captured but logged silently (line 141: `echo "[$(date)] Claude analysis failed (exit $exit_code)" >> "$LOG_FILE"`). If analysis fails, the loop continues without user notification. Observations file is archived regardless of success (line 147: `mv... 2>/dev/null || true`).
- **Severity**: **CRITICAL** — Pattern analysis failures silently swallowed; user never knows insights failed to generate.

**3. Observer startup with ignored shell errors (CRITICAL)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/agents/observer-loop.sh` (line 8)
- **Pattern**: `set +e` at the top of background observer loop
- **Issue**: `set +e` disables error checking for the entire background process. The comment (line 19) explains it's intentional to prevent claude CLI failures from killing the loop, but this also swallows errors in cleanup and setup. Line 182 has `|| echo "[$(date)] Warning: instinct prune failed (non-fatal)" >> "$LOG_FILE"` but many other commands have no fallback.
- **Severity**: **CRITICAL** — Background automation explicitly ignores errors.

**4. Unmonitored background observer with silent file operations (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (lines 149-154, 231-238, 349-350)
- **Pattern**: `find... -delete 2>/dev/null || true`, `mv... 2>/dev/null || true`, `rm -f... 2>/dev/null || true`
- **Issue**: Observation file archival, observation writes, and purge operations suppress all errors. If disk is full or permissions fail, no alert. Line 350: `nohup... start >/dev/null 2>&1 &` starts observer with no output capture.
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Silent data loss/archival failures.

**5. Subprocess calls without error checking (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/scripts/instinct-cli.py` (lines 140-147, 339-346)
- **Pattern**: `subprocess.run(...capture_output=True)` → check `returncode` but stderr ignored if non-zero
- **Issue**: Git operations fail silently; errors are only logged if detection succeeds. Line 146-147: `except FileNotFoundError: pass` (bare except with pass).
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Git operations can fail silently.

**6. Find with -delete and swallowed errors (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (line 152)
- **Pattern**: `find "${PROJECT_DIR}" -name "observations-*.jsonl" -mtime +30 -delete 2>/dev/null || true`
- **Issue**: File deletion suppresses all errors. If delete fails (permissions, filesystem issues), observation archive cleanup silently fails.
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Silent file operation failures.

---

### Important Findings

**7. Multiple `|| true` fallbacks without logging (IMPORTANT)**
- **Files**: Multiple shell scripts (observer-loop.sh, observe.sh, start-observer.sh, session-guardian.sh)
- **Count**: 43+ instances of `|| true`
- **Pattern**: `command || true` with no fallback action logged
- **Examples**:
  - `kill "$pid" 2>/dev/null || true` (lines 130, 137, 152, 405 in observe.sh) — fails silently
  - `mv... 2>/dev/null || true` (line 147, 237 in observe.sh) — archival failure not logged
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Silences failures that may indicate disk/permission issues.

**8. `2>/dev/null` without fallback (IMPORTANT)**
- **Files**: `observer-loop.sh`, `observe.sh`, `start-observer.sh`, `session-guardian.sh`
- **Count**: 20+ instances
- **Pattern**: `command 2>/dev/null` with no fallback or error logged
- **Examples**:
  - `kill -0 "$pid" 2>/dev/null` (line 128) — can't distinguish "process not running" from "kill failed"
  - `cat "$pid_file" 2>/dev/null` (lines 292-298 in observe.sh) — missing PID file not distinguished from read error
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Diagnostic information lost; can't distinguish missing files from permission errors.

**9. PID file validation insufficient (IMPORTANT)**
- **File**: `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` (lines 294-306)
- **Issue**: PID files are read and validated with regex, but if `cat` fails, error is silently ignored. Race conditions possible if PID file is deleted between check and read.
- **Severity**: **IMPORTANT** — Can signal wrong PID or stale zombie.

---

### Low-Risk Patterns (Acceptable)

**10. Intentional error suppression with clear rationale**
- **Files**: `scripts/codex-git-hooks/pre-commit` (line 38: `rg... 2>/dev/null`), `session-guardian.sh` (line 114: `2>/dev/null || true`)
- **Issue**: These are properly documented (comments explain why stderr is suppressed) and fall back to safe defaults.
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Acceptable trade-off.

**11. Tempfile cleanup with fallback**
- **Files**: `save-results.sh` (line 44), `scan-rules.sh` (line 28), `scan-skills.sh`
- **Pattern**: `trap 'rm -f "$tmp"' EXIT`
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Proper cleanup with trap handlers.

**12. Dry-run mode with explicit logging**
- **File**: `sync-ecc-to-codex.sh` (lines 44-52)
- **Pattern**: All operations logged/echoed, failures show up in output
- **Severity**: **LOW** — Good practice.

---

### Summary Table

| Category | Count | Severity | Actionable |
|----------|-------|----------|-----------|
| Unattended background tasks with suppressed errors | 4 | CRITICAL | Yes: Add logging to nohup invocations |
| Subprocess failures silently logged only | 2 | CRITICAL | Yes: Add stderr capture and alerting |
| Explicit error suppression (`set +e`) | 1 | CRITICAL | Yes: Narrow scope of `set +e` |
| File operations without diagnostics (`2>/dev/null`) | 20+ | IMPORTANT | Partial: Some acceptable, others need logging |
| `\|\| true` without logging | 43+ | IMPORTANT | Partial: Some acceptable, others need fallback |

---

### Recommendations

1. **Observer startup**: Replace `nohup ... >/dev/null 2>&1` with logging to file and stderr capture
2. **Claude analysis failures**: Add user-facing notification when analysis fails (not just logs)
3. **Narrow `set +e`**: Only disable errexit for specific commands that need it, not entire script
4. **File operations**: Log failures for archival, purge, and deletion operations
5. **PID file validation**: Add atomicity check or adopt a lock file instead</result>
